# LoCoBench-Agent Task

## Overview

**Task ID**: c_api_graphql_expert_079_cross_file_refactoring_expert_01
**Category**: cross_file_refactoring
**Difficulty**: expert
**Language**: c
**Context Length**: 1000845 tokens
**Files**: 84

## Task Title

Refactor Service-Level Error Handling into a Unified Common Library Abstraction

## Description

The SynestheticCanvas API Suite currently suffers from inconsistent error handling across its various microservices (palette, texture, audio, etc.). Each service defines its own error codes and formats, which are then manually and often incompletely translated into HTTP status codes at the API Gateway. This approach is brittle, hard to maintain, and leads to inconsistent error responses for the end-user. This task involves refactoring the error handling mechanism by creating a robust, unified error abstraction in the `sc_common` library and migrating the services to use it.

## Your Task

Your goal is to centralize and standardize error handling for the entire microservice suite.

**1. Enhance the Common Error Abstraction:**
   - In `libs/sc_common/include/sc_errors.h`, define a new structured error type, `sc_error_t`. This struct should contain:
     - An integer `code` (the service-specific error code).
     - A `char* message` (a detailed, dynamically allocated error message).
     - An enumeration `sc_service_domain_t` to identify the originating service (e.g., `SC_DOMAIN_PALETTE`, `SC_DOMAIN_TEXTURE`, etc.). You will need to define this enum.
     - An integer `http_status_code` (the recommended HTTP status to return, e.g., 404, 500).
   - In `sc_errors.h` and `sc_errors.c`, create and implement factory and destructor functions for this new type:
     - `sc_error_t* sc_error_create(sc_service_domain_t domain, int code, int http_status, const char* format, ...);` (variadic for easy message formatting)
     - `void sc_error_destroy(sc_error_t* err);`

**2. Refactor Core Services:**
   - Select two services for this refactoring: `palette-service` and `texture-service`.
   - Modify the function signatures within the service and repository layers (`palette_service.c`, `palette_repository.c`, `texture_service.c`, `texture_repository.c`) that currently return an integer error code. They should now return `sc_error_t*` on failure and `NULL` on success. You will need to update the function callers accordingly.
   - Replace all instances of ad-hoc error code returns (e.g., `return -1;`) with calls to your new `sc_error_create()` factory.

**3. Update the API Gateway:**
   - Modify the `api-gateway`'s service client (`api-gateway/src/services/service_client.c`) and fallback handlers (`api-gateway/src/rest/fallback_handlers.c`) to correctly interpret the new `sc_error_t*` returned from the services.
   - The gateway should no longer rely on simple integer codes. It must now use the `http_status_code` and `message` from the `sc_error_t` struct to generate the final HTTP response to the client.

**4. Update Tests:**
   - Modify the unit tests for the refactored services (`test_palette_service.c`, `test_texture_service.c`) to reflect the new function signatures and error handling logic. Tests that previously checked for integer return values like `-1` must now check for a non-NULL `sc_error_t*` and validate its contents.

**5. Build and Verify:**
   - Ensure the entire project, including the modified services, common library, and API gateway, compiles without warnings.
   - Ensure all updated tests pass.

## Expected Approach

An expert developer would approach this systematically:

1.  **Analyze and Design (Bottom-Up):**
    - Start by examining the existing error patterns in `palette_service.c` and `texture_service.c`. Note how errors (e.g., 'not found', 'database error') are currently represented.
    - Design the `sc_service_domain_t` enum and the `sc_error_t` struct in `libs/sc_common/include/sc_errors.h`.
    - Implement the `sc_error_create` and `sc_error_destroy` functions in `libs/sc_common/src/sc_errors.c`, paying close attention to dynamic memory allocation for the message string.

2.  **Refactor one service completely (`palette-service`):**
    - Start at the lowest level, likely `palette_repository.c`. Change function signatures from `int func(...)` to `sc_error_t* func(...)` where appropriate. Update the implementation to return `sc_error_create(...)` on failure.
    - Propagate these signature changes upwards into `palette_service.c` and then to `palette_handler.c`.
    - Update `test_palette_service.c` to align with the new error handling. Assert on the fields of the returned `sc_error_t` object in failure-case tests.
    - Compile and run the tests for this service to ensure it's working in isolation before proceeding.

3.  **Refactor the second service (`texture-service`):**
    - Repeat the process for `texture-service`, modifying its repository, service, handler, and test files.

4.  **Refactor the Consumer (`api-gateway`):**
    - Modify the functions in `service_client.c` that call the microservices. They now need to handle an `sc_error_t*` instead of a simple status code.
    - Update the generic error handling logic in `fallback_handlers.c` or `router.c` to unpack the `sc_error_t` object and use its `http_status_code` and `message` to build the final response.

5.  **Final Integration and Cleanup:**
    - Perform a full build of the entire `SynestheticCanvas` project using `scripts/build.sh`.
    - Run all test suites.
    - Review all changes for memory leaks (e.g., ensuring `sc_error_destroy` is called everywhere an error is handled and not propagated further).

## Evaluation Criteria

- **Correctness & Compilation:** The entire project must compile successfully without new warnings. All modified tests must pass, and no existing functionality should be broken.
- **Abstraction Quality:** The new `sc_error_t` abstraction in `sc_common` must be well-defined, and its helper functions must be correctly implemented, especially concerning memory management (e.g., `strdup` for the message, proper `free` in the destructor).
- **Refactoring Completeness:** Both `palette-service` and `texture-service` must be fully refactored to use the new error system, from the repository layer up to the handler.
- **Gateway Integration:** The API Gateway must correctly consume the new `sc_error_t` objects, using their fields to generate appropriate and consistent HTTP responses.
- **Test Adaptation:** Unit tests for the modified services must be updated to reflect the new function signatures and properly assert on the new error struct's contents.
- **Code Consistency:** The new error handling pattern must be applied consistently across all modified files.
- **Memory Safety:** The agent must correctly manage the lifecycle of `sc_error_t` objects, creating them on error and destroying them once handled to prevent memory leaks.

     1→/*
     2→ *  SynestheticCanvas API Suite - API Gateway
     3→ *  =========================================
     4→ *  File:    gateway_server.h
     5→ *  Author:  SynestheticCanvas Core Team
     6→ *
     7→ *  Description:
     8→ *      Public interface for the API-Gateway server.  The gateway is responsible
     9→ *      for brokering HTTP/2 REST endpoints, multiplexing GraphQL requests, and
    10→ *      enforcing cross-cutting concerns such as authentication, rate-limiting,
    11→ *      structured logging, and schema version negotiation.
    12→ *
    13→ *      This header intentionally exposes *only* the high-level orchestration
    14→ *      API—internals such as the concrete HTTP stack (libmicrohttpd, nghttp2,
    15→ *      or bespoke epoll loops) remain private so that the surrounding micro-
    16→ *      service constellation can be refactored without breaking dependants.
    17→ *
    18→ *  Usage:
    19→ *      #include <gateway_server.h>
    20→ *
    21→ *      gateway_cfg_t cfg = GATEWAY_CFG_INIT;
    22→ *      cfg.http_port  = 8080;
    23→ *      cfg.graphql_ws = true;
    24→ *
    25→ *      gateway_server_t *srv = gateway_server_create(&cfg, NULL);
    26→ *      if (!srv) {
    27→ *          fprintf(stderr, "Failed to bootstrap API-Gateway\n");
    28→ *          return EXIT_FAILURE;
    29→ *      }
    30→ *
    31→ *      if (gateway_server_start(srv) != GATEWAY_OK) {
    32→ *          gateway_server_destroy(srv);
    33→ *          return EXIT_FAILURE;
    34→ *      }
    35→ *
    36→ *      gateway_server_block(srv); // run until signalled
    37→ *      gateway_server_destroy(srv);

  - `/app/project/libs/sc_common/include/sc_logging.h` - Logging facilities
  - `/app/project/libs/sc_common/include/sc_types.h` - Common type definitions

- **Implementation Files:**
  - `/app/project/libs/sc_common/src/sc_errors.c` - Error code translations and management
  - `/app/project/libs/sc_common/src/sc_config.c` - Configuration handling
  - `/app/project/libs/sc_common/src/sc_logging.c` - Logging implementation

- **Build Config:** `/app/project/libs/sc_common/CMakeLists.txt`

     1→/*
     2→ * sc_errors.h
     3→ *
     4→ * Centralised error-handling utilities for the SynestheticCanvas micro-service
     5→ * constellation.  All public functions are re-entrant, thread-safe and can be
     6→ * used from C as well as C++ translation units.
     7→ *
     8→ * To provide the function *definitions* in a single translation unit, define
     9→ *
    10→ *      #define SC_ERRORS_IMPL
    11→ *
    12→ * **once** before including this header.  All other units should include the
    13→ * header without defining the macro, giving them static prototypes only.
    14→ *
    15→ * Example:
    16→ *      #define SC_ERRORS_IMPL
    17→ *      #include "sc_errors.h"
    18→ *
    19→ *      int main(void) {
    20→ *          ...
    21→ *      }

    10→ *          transport concerns via the Repository Pattern—callers inject a

    18→ *          Error handling: Each function returns an `sc_ps_status_t` which is
    19→ *          an enum of strongly-typed status codes.  No errno usage here.
    20→ *

/*
 * sc_errors.h
 *
 * Centralised error-handling utilities for the SynestheticCanvas micro-service
 * constellation.  All public functions are re-entrant, thread-safe and can be
 * used from C as well as C++ translation units.
 *
 * To provide the function *definitions* in a single translation unit, define
 *
 *      #define SC_ERRORS_IMPL
 *
 * **once** before including this header.  All other units should include the
 * header without defining the macro, giving them static prototypes only.
 *
 * Example:
 *      #define SC_ERRORS_IMPL
 *      #include "sc_errors.h"
 *
 *      int main(void) {
 *          ...
 *      }
 *
 * Copyright (c) 2024
 * SynestheticCanvas – All rights reserved.
 */

#ifndef SC_ERRORS_H
#define SC_ERRORS_H

/* ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
 * Public Includes
 * -------------------------------------------------------------------------*/
#include <errno.h>
#include <stdbool.h>
#include <stdint.h>
#include <stdio.h>
#include <stdlib.h> /* asprintf, malloc/free */
#include <string.h>

#if defined(__GNUC__) || defined(__clang__)
#   define SC_ATTR_FORMAT(archetype, string_index, first_to_check) \
        __attribute__((format(archetype, string_index, first_to_check)))
#else
#   define SC_ATTR_FORMAT(archetype, string_index, first_to_check)
#endif

#ifdef __cplusplus
extern "C" {
#endif

# Solution: Refactor Service-Level Error Handling into a Unified Common Library Abstraction

## Executive Summary

This document provides a complete solution for centralizing and standardizing error handling across the SynestheticCanvas microservice suite. The refactoring involves:

1. **Enhancing the Common Error Abstraction** in `libs/sc_common/`
2. **Refactoring the Palette Service** (`services/palette-service/`)
3. **Refactoring the Texture Service** (`services/texture-service/`)
4. **Updating the API Gateway** (`api-gateway/`)
5. **Updating Unit Tests**

## Analysis of Existing Error Handling

### Current State

After analyzing the codebase, I found the following error handling patterns:

1. **sc_common library** (`libs/sc_common/include/sc_errors.h`):
   - Already has an `sc_error_t` struct with `code`, `sys_err`, `msg`, `file`, `line`
   - Has an `sc_err_e` enumeration with comprehensive error codes
   - Has an `sc_err_to_http()` function that maps error codes to HTTP status codes
   - Uses macros like `SC_RAISE()` and `SC_TRY()` for error propagation
   - **Missing**: No service domain identification, no factory functions for dynamic error creation

2. **Palette Service** (`services/palette-service/`):
   - Uses `bool` return values for most functions
   - Has service-specific status enum `sc_ps_status_t` in the public header
   - Repository uses `palette_repo_status_t` enum
   - No unified error message propagation

3. **Texture Service** (`services/texture-service/`):
   - Uses `texture_service_status_t` enum

   - Handler functions consume errors and use `http_status_code` and `message` for responses

5. **Test Updates**:

   - Tests verify `sc_error_destroy()` is called to prevent leaks

This compilation unit\n * provides:\n *\n *  \u2022 A stable enumeration of error codes (mirrored in sc_errors.h).\n *  \u2022 Human-readable translations for each code (thread-safe, async-signal-safe).\n *  \u2022 Helper routines / macros for propagating and logging failures.\n *  \u2022 A lightweight, per-thread error context similar to errno, but extensible\n *    and service-aware.\n *\n * Copyright 2024\n * SPDX-License-Identifier: MIT\n */\n\n#include \"sc_errors.h\"        /* public interface */\n#include \"sc_log.h\"           /* internal logging facade */\n#include <pthread.h>\n#include <stdatomic.h>\n#include <stdio.h>\n#include <string.h>\n\n/* ============================================================================\n * Private constants / tables\n * ========================================================================== */\n\n/*\n * IMPORTANT: Keep the order in sync with enum sc_error_code in sc_errors.h.\n *\n * DO NOT insert values in the middle \u2013 always append, otherwise previously\n * serialized error codes will be reinterpreted.  Mark deprecated entries but\n * keep them in place.\n */\nstatic const char *const g_sc_error_lut[] = {\n    /* 0  */ \"Success\",\n    /* 1  */ \"Unknown failure\",\n    /* 2  */ \"Out of memory\",\n    /* 3  */ \"Null pointer dereference\",\n    /* 4  */ \"Invalid argument\",\n    /* 5  */ \"Index out of range\",\n    /* 6  */ \"Resource not found\",\n    /* 7  */ \"Permission denied\",\n    /* 8  */ \"Operation timed out\",\n    /* 9  */ \"Connection failed\",\n    /* 10 */ \"Protocol violation\",\n    /* 11 */ \"Data corruption detected\",\n    /* 12 */ \"Unimplemented feature\",\n    /* 13 */ \"Unsupported media type\",\n    /* 14 */ \"Configuration error\",\n    /* 15 */ \"I/O failure\",\n    /* 16 */ \"Filesystem full\",\n    /* 17 */ \"GraphQL validation error\",\n    /* 18 */ \"GraphQL execution error\",\n    /* 19 */ \"REST validation error\",\n    /* 20 */ \"Rate limit exceeded\",\n    /* 21 */ \"Service unavailable\",\n    /* 22 */ \"Schema version mismatch\",\n    /* 23 */ \"Database query failed\",\n    /* 24 */ \"Transaction aborted\",\n    /* 25 */ \"Threading error\",\n    /* 26 */ \"Serialization error\",\n    /* 27 */ \"Deserialization error\",\n    /* 28 */ \"Crypto / TLS error\",\n    /* 29 */ \"Cancellation requested\"\n};\n\n_Static_assert(SC_ERR__MAX == (sizeof g_sc_error_lut / sizeof g_sc_error_lut[0]),\n               \"g_sc_error_lut size must match sc_error_code enum\");\n\n/* ============================================================================\n * Per-thread errno implementation\n * ========================================================================== */\n\n/*\n * We keep the last error in a thread-local variable to avoid function signatures\n * exploding with additional parameters.  This should NOT be used for control\n * flow.  Instead, each function should return an explicit sc_error_code and let\n * callers inspect that directly.  The TLS value is useful as a \u201clast resort\u201d\n * when integrating with foreign code (e.g., gRPC, pthreads) that predates our\n * conventions.\n */\nstatic _Thread_local sc_error_code tl_last_error = SC_OK;\n\n/* -------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\nvoid sc_set_error(sc_error_code code)\n{\n    tl_last_error = code;\n}\n/* -------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\nsc_error_code sc_get_error(void)\n{\n    return tl_last_error;\n}\n/* ============================================================================\n * Public translation helpers\n * ========================================================================== */\n\nconst char *sc_error_to_cstr(sc_error_code code)\n{\n    if (code < 0 || code >= SC_ERR__MAX) {\n        return \"Invalid error code\"; /* Should never happen */\n    }\n    return g_sc_error_lut[code];\n}\n\n/* -------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n/*\n * A tiny, header-only logging wrapper could just format the message and forward\n * to sc_log_write().  Here we provide a convenience implementation so callers\n * can do:\n *\n *     if ((rc = sc_foo()) != SC_OK) {\n *         return sc_perror(rc, \"foo failed\");\n *     }\n */\nsc_error_code sc_perror(sc_error_code code, const char *context)\n{\n    const char *msg = sc_error_to_cstr(code);\n\n    if (context && *context) {\n        sc_log_write(SC_LOG_ERROR, \"[%s] %s\", context, msg);\n    } else {\n        sc_log_write(SC_LOG_ERROR, \"%s\", msg);\n    }\n\n    /* stash; do this after logging\u2014handlers may consult sc_get_error() */\n    sc_set_error(code);\n\n    return code;\n}\n\n/* ============================================================================\n * Extensibility: custom translators\n * ========================================================================== */\n\n/*\n * Some services may want to register a domain-specific mapping (e.g., map DB\n * vendor error codes into sc_error_code + additional diagnostics).  We expose a\n * simple listener pattern: interested parties register a callback that gets\n * invoked on every sc_set_error() and can perform their own side effects\n * (telemetry, tracing, etc.).\n */\n\n#define MAX_LISTENERS 8\n\ntypedef void (*sc_error_listener_fn)(sc_error_code code);\n\nstatic sc_error_listener_fn g_listeners[MAX_LISTENERS];\nstatic atomic_uint g_listener_count = 0;\n\n/* -------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\nbool sc_error_add_listener(sc_error_listener_fn fn)\n{\n    if (!fn)\n        return false;\n\n    unsigned idx = atomic_load_explicit(&g_listener_count, memory_order_relaxed);\n\n    if (idx >= MAX_LISTENERS)\n        return false;\n\n    g_listeners[idx] = fn;\n    atomic_fetch_add_explicit(&g_listener_count, 1, memory_order_release);\n    return true;\n}\n\n/* -------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\nvoid sc_error_notify(sc_error_code code)\n{\n    unsigned count = atomic_load_explicit(&g_listener_count, memory_order_acquire);\n\n    for (unsigned i = 0; i < count; ++i) {\n        if (g_listeners[i]) {\n            g_listeners[i](code);\n        }\n    }\n}\n\n/* -------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n/* Override default setter to broadcast events */\nvoid sc_set_error_broadcast(sc_error_code code)\n{\n    sc_set_error(code);        /* local TLS copy */\n    sc_error_notify(code);     /* fan out to listeners */\n}\n\n/* ============================================================================\n * Debug utilities\n * ========================================================================== */\n\n#ifdef SC_BUILD_DEBUG\n\n#include <inttypes.h>\n#include <stdlib.h>\n\nvoid sc_error_dump(FILE *fp)\n{\n    if (!fp) fp = stderr;\n\n    sc_error_code last = sc_get_error();\n    fprintf(fp, \"[dbg] last error = %d (%s)\\n\",\n            last, sc_error_to_cstr(last));\n}\n\n/*\n * Compile-time check that enum and LUT stay in sync,\n *   *and* catch duplicate values.\n */\nstatic void sc_error_compile_asserts(void)\n{\n    for (int i = 0; i < SC_ERR__MAX; ++i) {\n        /* This branchless trick will abort at run-time if duplicates detected.\n         * Not perfect, but still helps to catch copy-paste mistakes.\n         */\n        for (int j = i + 1; j < SC_ERR__MAX; ++j) {\n            if (strcmp(g_sc_error_lut[i], g_sc_error_lut[j]) == 0) {\n                fprintf(stderr,\n                        \"sc_errors: duplicate error string \\\"%s\\\" @ %d and %d\\n\",\n                        g_sc_error_lut[i], i, j);\n                abort();\n            }\n        }\n    }\n}\n/* Run once at startup */\n__attribute__((constructor))\nstatic void sc_error_init_ctor(void)\n{\n    sc_error_compile_asserts();\n}\n\n#endif /* SC_BUILD_DEBUG */\n\n/* ============================================================================\n * End of file\n * ========================================================================== */\n",

i < sizeof statements / sizeof statements[0]; ++i) {\n        int rc = sqlite3_prepare_v2(repo->db,\n                                    statements[i].sql,\n                                    -1,\n                                    statements[i].stmt,\n                                    NULL);\n        if (rc != SQLITE_OK) {\n            LOG_ERROR(\"Failed to compile statement (%zu): %s\",\n                      i,\n                      sqlite3_errmsg(repo->db));\n            return PAL_REPO_STORAGE_ERROR;\n        }\n    }\n    return PAL_REPO_OK;\n}\n\nstatic void\nrepository_finalize_statements(struct palette_repository *repo)\n{\n    if (!repo) {\n        return;\n    }\n    sqlite3_finalize(repo->stmt_get_by_id);\n    sqlite3_finalize(repo->stmt_list_paginated);\n    sqlite3_finalize(repo->stmt_insert);\n    sqlite3_finalize(repo->stmt_update);\n    sqlite3_finalize(repo->stmt_delete);\n}\n\n/* -------------------------------------------------------------------------\n * End of file\n * ------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n```",

Converts an incoming request into an internal\n * representation, performs route lookup, validation, and hands control to the\n * endpoint handler.  Returns `true` if a route was matched (regardless of\n * HTTP status).  Returns `false` when no route matched, allowing the caller to\n * fall back to 404 behavior.\n */\nbool sc_router_handle(sc_router_t        *router,\n                      const sc_http_request_t  *req,\n                      sc_http_response_t       *res)\n{\n    if (!router || !req || !res)\n        return false;\n\n    for (size_t i = 0;              char *err_buf, size_t err_len)\n{\n    char regex_buf[ROUTER_MAX_REGEX] = {0};\n    char *dst = regex_buf;\n    const char *src = pattern;\n\n    if (*src != '/')\n    {\n Extract params into key/value vector (already matched!) */\nstatic bool extract_params(const route_t   *route,\n                           const char      *path,\n                           sc_param_list_t *out)\n{\n    size_t groups   = route->param_names.len;\n    regmatch_t      match[groups + 1]; /* group 0 = whole match */\n\n    if (regexec(&route->regex, path, groups + 1, match, 0) != 0)\n        return false;\n\n    for (size_t i = 0; i < groups; ++i)\n    {\n        if (match[i + 1].rm_so == -1)\n            continue; /* shouldn't happen */\n\n        size_t len = (size_t)(match[i + 1].rm_eo - match[i + 1].rm_so);\n        char *value = strndup(path + match[i + 1].rm_so, len);\n        sc_param_list_add(out, route->param_names.items[i], value);\n \u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500 */\n/*                           Worker Thread Logic                             */\n/* \u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500 */\n\ntypedef struct {\n    build_ctx_t *ctx;\n    size_t       index; /* 0-based index into ctx->services */\n} worker_arg_t;\n\nstatic void *builder_thread(void *arg_void)\n{\n    worker_arg_t *arg = arg_void;\n    build_ctx_t  *ctx = arg->ctx;\n    service_t    *svc = &ctx->services[arg->index];\n\n    if (!svc->needs_build) {\n        /* No work */\n        svc->result = 0;\n        return NULL;\n    }\n\n    char cmdline[PATH_MAX + 64];\n    /* Example build command: make -C /abs/path VERBOSE=1 */\n    snprintf(cmdline, sizeof cmdline,\n             \"%s -C \\\"%s\\\" %s%s\",\n             ctx->build_cmd,\n             svc->dir,\n             ctx->verbose ? \"VERBOSE=1 \" : \"\",\n             \"all\");\n\n    info(\"%s \u2011 %s\", timestamp(), cmdline);\n\n    int rc = system(cmdline);\n    if (rc == -1) {\n        err(\"%s \u2011 failed to spawn: %s\", timestamp(), strerror(errno));\n        svc->result = 127;\n    } else {\n        svc->result = WEXITSTATUS(rc);\n        if (svc->result == 0)\n            success(\"%s \u2011 built successfully\", timestamp());\n        else\n            err(\"%s \u2011 build failed with %d\", timestamp(), svc->result);\n    }\n\n    return NULL;\n}\n\n/* \u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500 */\n/*                           High-Level Build API                            */\n/* \u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500 */\n\nstatic void schedule_builds(build_ctx_t *ctx)\n{\n    /* Simple static thread pool (one per service or limited by parallelism) */\n    size_t workers = ctx->count < (size_t)ctx->parallelism ? ctx->count\n                                                           : (size_t)ctx->parallelism;\n    pthread_t *threads = calloc(workers, sizeof *threads);\n\n    size_t next_job = 0;\n    size_t active   = 0;\n\n    while (next_job < ctx->count || active) {\n        /* Spawn new threads while we have capacity */\n        while (active < workers && next_job < ctx->count) {\n            worker_arg_t *arg = calloc(1, sizeof *arg);\n            arg->ctx   = ctx;\n            arg->index = next_job++;\n\n            if (pthread_create(&threads[active], NULL, builder_thread, arg) != 0) {\n                err(\"pthread_create failed: %s\", strerror(errno));\n                free(arg);\n                continue;\n            }\n            active++;\n        }\n\n        /* Wait for any thread to finish */\n        for (size_t i = 0; i < active; ++i) {\n            if (threads[i] && pthread_tryjoin_np /* GNU extension */) ; /* NOOP */\n        }\n\n        /* Collapse finished thread slots */\n        size_t write = 0;\n        for (size_t read = 0; read < active; ++read) {\n            if (threads[read] == 0) /* vacant */\n                continue;\n            if (pthread_tryjoin_np(threads[read], NULL) == 0) {\n                threads[read] = 0;\n            } else {\n                threads[write++] = threads[read];\n            }\n        }\n        active = write;\n\n        if (g_cancel_requested) {\n            warn(\"Cancelling remaining builds due to signal\");\n            break;\n        }\n\n        /* Small sleep to avoid busy loop */\n        struct timespec ts = {.tv_sec = 0, .tv_nsec = 100000000}; /* 100ms */\n        nanosleep(&ts, NULL);\n    }\n\n    free(threads);\n}\n\n/* Returns non-zero if any service\u2019s *.c sources are newer than \u201cbuild/.stamp\u201d */\nstatic bool service_needs_rebuild(const char *service_dir)\n{\n    char stamp[PATH_MAX];\n    join_path(stamp, sizeof stamp, service_dir, \"build/.stamp\");\n\n    time_t stamp_time = mtime_of(stamp);\n    if (stamp_time == 0)\n        return true; /* never built */\n\n    /* Na\u00efve heuristic: if any *.c changed, rebuild */\n    char src_glob[PATH_MAX];\n    join_path(src_glob, sizeof src_glob, service_dir, \"src\");\n\n    /* For portability, walk using \u201cfind\u201d + \u201cstat\u201d instead of <fts.h> */\n    char find_cmd[PATH_MAX + 64];\n    snprintf(find_cmd, sizeof find_cmd,\n             \"find \\\"%s\\\" -name '*.c' -newer \\\"%s\\\" -print -quit 2>/dev/null\",\n             src_glob, stamp);\n\n    int rc = system(find_cmd);\n    return rc == 0; /* return 0 if match found \u21d2 needs rebuild */\n}\n\n/* \u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500 */\n/*                                   Main                                    */\n/* \u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500 */\n\nint main(int argc, char **argv)\n{\n    /* ------------------------------------------------------------ */\n    /* 1. Register signal handlers                                  */\n    struct sigaction sa = {.sa_handler = on_signal};\n    sigaction(SIGINT,  &sa, NULL);\n    sigaction(SIGTERM, &sa, NULL);\n\n    /* ------------------------------------------------------------ */\n    /* 2. Default config                                            */\n    build_ctx_t ctx = {\n        .parallelism = DEFAULT_PARALLELISM,\n        .verbose     = false,\n        .build_cmd   = \"make\"\n    };\n\n    /* ------------------------------------------------------------ */\n    /* 3. CLI parse                                                 */\n    bool all_flag    = true;\n    char single_service[PATH_MAX] = {0};\n    bool clean_flag  = false;\n\n    for (int i = 1; i < argc; ++i) {\n        if (!strcmp(argv[i], \"--all\")) {\n            all_flag = true;\n        } else if (!strcmp(argv[i], \"--service\") && i + 1 < argc) {\n            strncpy(single_service, argv[++i], sizeof single_service - 1);\n            all_flag = false;\n        } else if (!strcmp(argv[i], \"--clean\")) {\n            clean_flag = true;\n        } else if ((!strcmp(argv[i], \"-j\") || !strcmp(argv[i], \"--jobs\")) && i + 1 < argc) {\n            ctx.parallelism = atoi(argv[++i]);\n        } else if (!strcmp(argv[i], \"--verbose\")) {\n            ctx.verbose = true;\n        } else if (!strcmp(argv[i], \"-h\") || !strcmp(argv[i], \"--help\")) {\n            print_usage(argv[0]);\n            return EXIT_SUCCESS;\n        } else {\n            err(\"Unknown option: %s\", argv[i]);\n            print_usage(argv[0]);\n            return EXIT_FAILURE;\n        }\n    }\n\n    /* ------------------------------------------------------------ */\n    /* 4. Find repository root                                      */\n    char repo_root[PATH_MAX];\n    if (!find_repo_root(repo_root, sizeof repo_root)) {\n        err(\"Unable to locate repository root \u2013 are you inside SynestheticCanvas?\");\n        return EXIT_FAILURE;\n    }\n    info(\"Repository root detected at %s\", repo_root);\n    if (chdir(repo_root) != 0) {\n        err(\"chdir to repo root failed: %s\", strerror(errno));\n        return EXIT_FAILURE;\n    }\n\n    /* ------------------------------------------------------------ */\n    /* 5. Enumerate services                                        */\n    size_t svc_count = 0;\n    for (const char **p = DEFAULT_SERVICES; *p; ++p)\n        svc_count++;\n\n    ctx.services = calloc(svc_count, sizeof *ctx.services);\n    ctx.count    = svc_count;\n\n    for (size_t i = 0; i < svc_count; ++i) {\n        join_path(ctx.services[i].dir, sizeof ctx.services[i].dir,\n                  repo_root, DEFAULT_SERVICES[i]);\n        if (!all_flag) {\n            char *leaf = strrchr(ctx.services[i].dir, '/');\n            if (leaf && strcmp(leaf + 1, single_service) != 0) {\n                ctx.services[i].needs_build = false;\n                continue;\n            }\n        }\n\n        /* Clean if requested */\n        if (clean_flag) {\n            char clean_cmd[PATH_MAX + 32];\n            snprintf(clean_cmd, sizeof clean_cmd,\n                     \"%s -C \\\"%s\\\" clean\", ctx.build_cmd, ctx.services[i].dir);\n            info(\"Cleaning %s\", ctx.services[i].dir);\n            system(clean_cmd);\n        }\n\n        ctx.services[i].needs_build = service_needs_rebuild(ctx.services[i].dir);\n    }\n\n    /* ------------------------------------------------------------ */\n    /* 6. Execute builds                                            */\n    schedule_builds(&ctx);\n\n    /* ------------------------------------------------------------ */\n    /* 7. Summarise results                                         */\n    int exit_code = 0;\n    for (size_t i = 0; i < ctx.count; ++i) {\n        const service_t *svc = &ctx.services[i];\n        if (!svc->needs_build)\n            continue;\n\n        if (svc->result == 0) {\n            success(\"%s \u2011 %s built OK\", timestamp(), svc->dir);\n        } else {\n            err(\"%s \u2011 %s failed\", timestamp(), svc->dir);\n            exit_code = 1;\n        }\n    }\n\n    if (g_cancel_requested)\n        exit_code = 130; /* typical exit code for SIGINT */\n\n    free(ctx.services);\n    return exit_code;\n}\n```",

  "content": "# Solution: Refactor Service-Level Error Handling into a Unified Common Library Abstraction\n\n## Executive Summary\n\nThis document provides a complete solution for centralizing and standardizing error handling across the SynestheticCanvas microservice suite. The refactoring involves:\n\n1. **Enhancing the Common Error Abstraction** in `libs/sc_common/`\n2. **Refactoring the Palette Service** (`services/palette-service/`)\n3. **Refactoring the Texture Service** (`services/texture-service/`)\n4. **Updating the API Gateway** (`api-gateway/`)\n5. **Updating Unit Tests**\n\n## Analysis of Existing Error Handling\n\n### Current State\n\nAfter analyzing the codebase, I found the following error handling patterns:\n\n1. **sc_common library** (`libs/sc_common/include/sc_errors.h`):\n   - Already has an `sc_error_t` struct with `code`, `sys_err`, `msg`, `file`, `line`\n   - Has an `sc_err_e` enumeration with comprehensive error codes\n   - Has an `sc_err_to_http()` function that maps error codes to HTTP status codes\n   - Uses macros like `SC_RAISE()` and `SC_TRY()` for error propagation\n   - **Missing**: No service domain identification, no factory functions for dynamic error creation\n\n2. **Palette Service** (`services/palette-service/`):\n   - Uses `bool` return values for most functions\n   - Has service-specific status enum `sc_ps_status_t` in the public header\n   - Repository uses `palette_repo_status_t` enum\n   - No unified error message propagation\n\n3. **Texture Service** (`services/texture-service/`):\n   - Uses `texture_service_status_t` enum\n   - Repository uses integer codes (`REPO_OK`, `REPO_ERR_*`)\n   - No unified error message propagation\n\n4. **API Gateway** (`api-gateway/`):\n   - Service client uses simple integer return codes\n   - Fallback handlers generate JSON error responses manually\n   - No structured consumption of service errors\n\n## Implementation Plan\n\n### 1. Enhanced Common Error Abstraction\n\n#### Changes to `libs/sc_common/include/sc_errors.h`\n\nAdd the following after the existing includes and before the error enumeration:\n\n```c\n/* ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n * Service domain enumeration\n * Identifies the originating service for unified error handling across\n * the microservice constellation.\n * -------------------------------------------------------------------------*/\ntypedef enum {\n    SC_DOMAIN_UNKNOWN = 0,\n    SC_DOMAIN_COMMON,         /* Common library errors */\n    SC_DOMAIN_PALETTE,        /* Palette service */\n    SC_DOMAIN_TEXTURE,        /* Texture service */\n    SC_DOMAIN_AUDIO,          /* Audio service */\n    SC_DOMAIN_NARRATIVE,      /* Narrative service */\n    SC_DOMAIN_GATEWAY         /* API Gateway */\n} sc_service_domain_t;\n```\n\nModify the existing `sc_error_t` struct to include domain and HTTP status:\n\n```c\n/* ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n * Structured error object (enhanced)\n * -------------------------------------------------------------------------*/\ntypedef struct sc_error {\n    sc_err_e             code;            /* High level error code */\n    int                  sys_err;         /* Underlying errno / subsystem code */\n    sc_service_domain_t  domain;          /* Originating service domain */\n    int                  http_status_code;/* Recommended HTTP status code */\n    char                *message;         /* Dynamically allocated, human-readable text */\n    const char          *file;            /* Source file where error was raised */\n    int                  line;            /* Line in source file */\n} sc_error_t;\n\n#define SC_ERROR_INIT { \\\n    .code = SC_OK, \\\n    .sys_err = 0, \\\n    .domain = SC_DOMAIN_UNKNOWN, \\\n    .http_status_code = 200, \\\n    .message = NULL, \\\n    .file = NULL, \\\n    .line = 0 \\\n}\n```\n\nAdd factory and destructor function declarations:\n\n```c\n/* ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n * Error factory and destructor functions\n * -------------------------------------------------------------------------*/\n\n/**\n * sc_error_create\n *\n * Factory function to create a new sc_error_t instance with all fields populated.\n * The message is formatted using printf-style variadic arguments.\n *\n * @param domain      The originating service domain\n * @param code        The service-specific error code\n * @param http_status The recommended HTTP status code to return\n * @param format      Printf-style format string for the error message\n * @param ...         Format arguments\n *\n * @return Pointer to a heap-allocated sc_error_t, or NULL on allocation failure.\n *         Caller must free with sc_error_destroy().\n */\nsc_error_t* sc_error_create(sc_service_domain_t domain,\n                            int code,\n                            int http_status,\n                            const char* format, ...) SC_ATTR_FORMAT(printf, 4, 5);\n\n/**\n * sc_error_create_v\n *\n * Variadic list version of sc_error_create for internal use.\n */\nsc_error_t* sc_error_create_v(sc_service_domain_t domain,\n                              int code,\n                              int http_status,\n                              const char* format,\n                              va_list args);\n\n/**\n * sc_error_destroy\n *\n * Frees all resources associated with an sc_error_t instance.\n * Safe to call with NULL.\n *\n * @param err The error to destroy\n */\nvoid sc_error_destroy(sc_error_t* err);\n\n/**\n * sc_error_get_domain_name\n *\n * Returns a human-readable string for the service domain.\n */\nconst char* sc_error_get_domain_name(sc_service_domain_t domain);\n```\n\n#### Implementation in `libs/sc_common/src/sc_errors.c`\n\nAdd implementations after the existing code:\n\n```c\n/* ============================================================================\n * Domain name lookup table\n * ========================================================================== */\n\nstatic const char* const g_domain_names[] = {\n    [SC_DOMAIN_UNKNOWN]   = \"unknown\",\n    [SC_DOMAIN_COMMON]    = \"common\",\n    [SC_DOMAIN_PALETTE]   = \"palette-service\",\n    [SC_DOMAIN_TEXTURE]   = \"texture-service\",\n    [SC_DOMAIN_AUDIO]     = \"audio-service\",\n    [SC_DOMAIN_NARRATIVE] = \"narrative-service\",\n    [SC_DOMAIN_GATEWAY]   = \"api-gateway\"\n};\n\nconst char* sc_error_get_domain_name(sc_service_domain_t domain)\n{\n    if (domain < 0 || domain > SC_DOMAIN_GATEWAY) {\n        return \"invalid-domain\";\n    }\n    return g_domain_names[domain];\n}\n\n/* ============================================================================\n * Error factory implementation\n * ========================================================================== */\n\nsc_error_t* sc_error_create_v(sc_service_domain_t domain,\n                              int code,\n                              int http_status,\n                              const char* format,\n                              va_list args)\n{\n    sc_error_t* err = calloc(1, sizeof(sc_error_t));\n    if (!err) {\n        return NULL;\n    }\n\n    err->domain = domain;\n    err->code = (sc_err_e)code;\n    err->http_status_code = http_status;\n    err->sys_err = errno;  /* Capture current errno */\n    err->file = NULL;\n    err->line = 0;\n\n    /* Format the message if format string provided */\n    if (format != NULL) {\n        va_list args_copy;\n        va_copy(args_copy, args);\n        int len = vsnprintf(NULL, 0, format, args_copy);\n        va_end(args_copy);\n\n        if (len > 0) {\n            err->message = malloc((size_t)len + 1);\n            if (err->message) {\n                vsnprintf(err->message, (size_t)len + 1, format, args);\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    return err;\n}\n\nsc_error_t* sc_error_create(sc_service_domain_t domain,\n                            int code,\n                            int http_status,\n                            const char* format, ...)\n{\n    va_list args;\n    va_start(args, format);\n    sc_error_t* err = sc_error_create_v(domain, code, http_status, format, args);\n    va_end(args);\n    return err;\n}\n\nvoid sc_error_destroy(sc_error_t* err)\n{\n    if (err == NULL) {\n        return;\n    }\n\n    /* Free the dynamically allocated message */\n    if (err->message != NULL) {\n        free(err->message);\n        err->message = NULL;\n    }\n\n    /* Free the error struct itself */\n    free(err);\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n### 2. sc_service_response_free(sc_service_response_t *resp);\n\n/**\n * Enhanced call function that returns structured errors\n */\nint sc_service_client_call_ex(sc_service_client_t     *cli,\n                              sc_service_endp_t        endpoint,\n                              const char              *method,\n                              const char              *path,\n                              const char              *request_json,\n                              sc_service_response_t   *response);\n```\n\n#### Changes to `api-gateway/src/services/service_client.c`\n\n```c\n#include \"sc_errors.h\"\n\nvoid sc_service_response_free(sc_service_response_t *resp)\n{\n    if (!resp) return;\n\n    if (resp->body) {\n        cJSON_Delete(resp->body);\n        resp->body = NULL;\n    request_json, &body_json, &http_status);\n\n    response->http_status = http_status;\n    response->body = body_json;\n\n    if (rc != SC_OK) {\n        response->status = rc;\n                              \"%s\", err_msg);\n            response->status = err_code;\n            return err_code;\n        }\n    }\n\n    response->status = SC_OK;\n    return *json = cJSON_PrintUnformatted(root);\n    cJSON_Delete(root);\n    return json;\n}\n\n/* New handler for service errors */\nRestResponse\nrest_fallback_service_error(const RestRequest *req,\n                            const sc_error_t  *err)\n{\n    LOG_DEBUG(\"[REST] Service error handler for URI '%s': %s\",\n              req->uri, err ? err->message : \"null error\");\n\n    char *payload = build_error_from_sc_error(err);\n\n    RestResponse res = {\n        .status_code  = err ? err->http_status_code : 500,\n        .content_type = MIME_APP_JSON,\n        .body         = payload,\n        .body_len     = strlen(payload),\n        .must_free    = true\n    };\n    return res;\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n### 5. Errors\n\nErrors are created using `sc_error_create()` which allocates:\n1. The `sc_error_t` struct itself\n2. A copy of the formatted message string\n\n```c\nsc_error_t* err = sc_error_create(SC_DOMAIN_PALETTE, SC_ERR_DATA_NOT_FOUND, 404,\n                                  \"Palette with id %s not found\", id);\n```\n\n### Destroying Errors\n\nErrors must be destroyed when no longer needed to prevent memory leaks:\n\n```c\nif (err != NULL) {\n    /* Handle the error */\n    log_error(\"Error: %s\", err->message);\n\n    /* Destroy when done */\n    sc_error_destroy(err);\n}\n```\n\n### Error Propagation\n\nWhen propagating errors up the call stack, the caller takes ownership:\n\n```c\nsc_error_t* do_operation(void) {\n    sc_error_t* err = some_lower_level_call();\n    if (err != NULL) {\n        /* Add context and return - caller now owns the error */\n        return err;\n    }\n    return NULL;  /* Success */\n}\n```\n\n### Error Handling Pattern\n\nThe recommended pattern for consuming functions:\n\n```c\nvoid handle_request(Request* req, Response* resp) {\n    sc_error_t* err = service_operation(req->data);\n\n    if (err != NULL) {\n        /* Use error details to build response */\n        resp->status = err->http_status_code;\n        resp->body = format_error_json(err);\n\n        /* Destroy the error after use */\n        sc_error_destroy(err);\n        return;\n    }\n\n    /* Success path */\n    resp->status = 200;\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## Build Instructions\n\nAfter implementing all changes:\n\n```bash\n# From project root\nmkdir -p build && cd build\ncmake .. -DCMAKE_BUILD_TYPE=Debug -DSC_ENABLE_TESTS=ON\nmake -j$(nproc)\n\n# Run tests\nctest --output-on-failure\n```\n\nOr using the build script:\n\n```bash\n./scripts/build.sh --all --verbose\n```\n\n---\n\n## Summary of Changes by File\n\n| File | Changes   "content": "# Solution: Refactor Service-Level Error Handling into a Unified Common Library Abstraction\n\n## Executive Summary\n\nThis document provides a complete solution for centralizing and standardizing error handling across the SynestheticCanvas microservice suite. The refactoring involves:\n\n1. **Enhancing the Common Error Abstraction** in `libs/sc_common/`\n2. **Refactoring the Palette Service** (`services/palette-service/`)\n3. **Refactoring the Texture Service** (`services/texture-service/`)\n4. **Updating the API Gateway** (`api-gateway/`)\n5. **Updating Unit Tests**\n\n## Analysis of Existing Error Handling\n\n### Current State\n\nAfter analyzing the codebase, I found the following error handling patterns:\n\n1. **sc_common library** (`libs/sc_common/include/sc_errors.h`):\n   - Already has an `sc_error_t` struct with `code`, `sys_err`, `msg`, `file`, `line`\n   - Has an `sc_err_e` enumeration with comprehensive error codes\n   - Has an `sc_err_to_http()` function that maps error codes to HTTP status codes\n   - Uses macros like `SC_RAISE()` and `SC_TRY()` for error propagation\n   - **Missing**: No service domain identification, no factory functions for dynamic error creation\n\n2. **Palette Service** (`services/palette-service/`):\n   - Uses `bool` return values for most functions\n   - Has service-specific status enum `sc_ps_status_t` in the public header\n   - Repository uses `palette_repo_status_t` enum\n   - No unified error message propagation\n\n3. **Texture Service** (`services/texture-service/`):\n   - Uses `texture_service_status_t` enum\n   - Repository uses integer codes (`REPO_OK`, `REPO_ERR_*`)\n   - No unified error message propagation\n\n4. **API Gateway** (`api-gateway/`):\n   - Service client uses simple integer return codes\n   - Fallback handlers generate JSON error responses manually\n   - No structured consumption of service errors\n\n## Implementation Plan\n\n### 1. Enhanced Common Error Abstraction\n\n#### Changes to `libs/sc_common/include/sc_errors.h`\n\nAdd the following after the existing includes and before the error enumeration:\n\n```c\n/* ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n * Service domain enumeration\n * Identifies the originating service for unified error handling across\n * the microservice constellation.\n * -------------------------------------------------------------------------*/\ntypedef enum {\n    SC_DOMAIN_UNKNOWN = 0,\n    SC_DOMAIN_COMMON,         /* Common library errors */\n    SC_DOMAIN_PALETTE,        /* Palette service */\n    SC_DOMAIN_TEXTURE,        /* Texture service */\n    SC_DOMAIN_AUDIO,          /* Audio service */\n    SC_DOMAIN_NARRATIVE,      /* Narrative service */\n    SC_DOMAIN_GATEWAY         /* API Gateway */\n} sc_service_domain_t;\n```\n\nModify the existing `sc_error_t` struct to include domain and HTTP status:\n\n```c\n/* ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n * Structured error object (enhanced)\n * -------------------------------------------------------------------------*/\ntypedef struct sc_error {\n    sc_err_e             code;            /* High level error code */\n    int                  sys_err;         /* Underlying errno / subsystem code */\n    sc_service_domain_t  domain;          /* Originating service domain */\n    int                  http_status_code;/* Recommended HTTP status code */\n    char                *message;         /* Dynamically allocated, human-readable text */\n    const char          *file;            /* Source file where error was raised */\n    int                  line;            /* Line in source file */\n} sc_error_t;\n\n#define SC_ERROR_INIT { \\\n    .code = SC_OK, \\\n    .sys_err = 0, \\\n    .domain = SC_DOMAIN_UNKNOWN, \\\n    .http_status_code = 200, \\\n    .message = NULL, \\\n    .file = NULL, \\\n    .line = 0 \\\n}\n```\n\nAdd factory and destructor function declarations:\n\n```c\n/* ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n * Error factory and destructor functions\n * -------------------------------------------------------------------------*/\n\n/**\n * sc_error_create\n *\n * Factory function to create a new sc_error_t instance with all fields populated.\n * The message is formatted using printf-style variadic arguments.\n *\n * @param domain      The originating service domain\n * @param code        The service-specific error code\n * @param http_status The recommended HTTP status code to return\n * @param format      Printf-style format string for the error message\n * @param ...         Format arguments\n *\n * @return Pointer to a heap-allocated sc_error_t, or NULL on allocation failure.\n *         Caller must free with sc_error_destroy().\n */\nsc_error_t* sc_error_create(sc_service_domain_t domain,\n                            int code,\n                            int http_status,\n                            const char* format, ...) SC_ATTR_FORMAT(printf, 4, 5);\n\n/**\n * sc_error_create_v\n *\n * Variadic list version of sc_error_create for internal use.\n */\nsc_error_t* sc_error_create_v(sc_service_domain_t domain,\n                              int code,\n                              int http_status,\n                              const char* format,\n                              va_list args);\n\n/**\n * sc_error_destroy\n *\n * Frees all resources associated with an sc_error_t instance.\n * Safe to call with NULL.\n *\n * @param err The error to destroy\n */\nvoid sc_error_destroy(sc_error_t* err);\n\n/**\n * sc_error_get_domain_name\n *\n * Returns a human-readable string for the service domain.\n */\nconst char* sc_error_get_domain_name(sc_service_domain_t domain);\n```\n\n#### Implementation in `libs/sc_common/src/sc_errors.c`\n\nAdd implementations after the existing code:\n\n```c\n/* ============================================================================\n * Domain name lookup table\n * ========================================================================== */\n\nstatic const char* const g_domain_names[] = {\n    [SC_DOMAIN_UNKNOWN]   = \"unknown\",\n    [SC_DOMAIN_COMMON]    = \"common\",\n    [SC_DOMAIN_PALETTE]   = \"palette-service\",\n    [SC_DOMAIN_TEXTURE]   = \"texture-service\",\n    [SC_DOMAIN_AUDIO]     = \"audio-service\",\n    [SC_DOMAIN_NARRATIVE] = \"narrative-service\",\n    [SC_DOMAIN_GATEWAY]   = \"api-gateway\"\n};\n\nconst char* sc_error_get_domain_name(sc_service_domain_t domain)\n{\n    if (domain < 0 || domain > SC_DOMAIN_GATEWAY) {\n        return \"invalid-domain\";\n    }\n    return g_domain_names[domain];\n}\n\n/* ============================================================================\n * Error factory implementation\n * ========================================================================== */\n\nsc_error_t* sc_error_create_v(sc_service_domain_t domain,\n                              int code,\n                              int http_status,\n                              const char* format,\n                              va_list args)\n{\n    sc_error_t* err = calloc(1, sizeof(sc_error_t));\n    if (!err) {\n        return NULL;\n    }\n\n    err->domain = domain;\n    err->code = (sc_err_e)code;\n    err->http_status_code = http_status;\n    err->sys_err = errno;  /* Capture current errno */\n    err->file = NULL;\n    err->line = 0;\n\n    /* Format the message if format string provided */\n    if (format != NULL) {\n        va_list args_copy;\n        va_copy(args_copy, args);\n        int len = vsnprintf(NULL, 0, format, args_copy);\n        va_end(args_copy);\n\n        if (len > 0) {\n            err->message = malloc((size_t)len + 1);\n            if (err->message) {\n                vsnprintf(err->message, (size_t)len + 1, format, args);\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    return err;\n}\n\nsc_error_t* sc_error_create(sc_service_domain_t domain,\n                            int code,\n                            int http_status,\n                            const char* format, ...)\n{\n    va_list args;\n    va_start(args, format);\n    sc_error_t* err = sc_error_create_v(domain, code, http_status, format, args);\n    va_end(args);\n    return err;\n}\n\nvoid sc_error_destroy(sc_error_t* err)\n{\n    if (err == NULL) {\n        return;\n    }\n\n    /* Free the dynamically allocated message */\n    if (err->message != NULL) {\n        free(err->message);\n        err->message = NULL;\n    }\n\n    /* Free the error struct itself */\n    free(err);\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n### 2.                 sc_service_endp_t        endpoint,\n                              const char              *method,\n                              const char              *path,\n                              const char              *request_json,\n                              sc_service_response_t   *response);\n```\n\n#### Changes to `api-gateway/src/services/service_client.c`\n\n```c\n#include \"sc_errors.h\"\n\nvoid sc_service_response_free(sc_service_response_t *resp)\n{\n    if (!resp) return;\n\n    if (resp->body) {\n        cJSON_Delete(resp->body);\n        resp->body = NULL;\n    }\n\n    if (resp->error) {\n        sc_error_destroy(resp->error);\n        resp->error = NULL;\n    }\n}\n\nint sc_service_client_call_ex(sc_service_client_t     *cli,\n                              sc_service_endp_t        endpoint,\n                              const char              *method,\n                              const char              *path,\n                              const char              *request_json,\n                              sc_service_response_t   *response)\n{\n    if (!cli || !method || !path || !response) {\n        return SC_EINVAL;\n    }\n\n    memset(response, 0, sizeof(*response));\n\n    cJSON *body_json = NULL;\n    long http_status = 0;\n\n    int rc = sc_service_client_call(cli, endpoint, method, path,\n                                    request_json, &body_json, &http_status);\n\n    response->http_status = http_status;\n    response->body = body_json;\n\n    if (rc != SC_OK) {\n        response->status = rc;\n        response->error = sc_error_create(SC_DOMAIN_GATEWAY, rc, (int)http_status,\n                                          \"Service call failed with status %ld\", http_status);\n        return rc;\n    }\n\n    /* Check if the response body contains an error structure */\n    if (body_json) {\n        cJSON *error_obj = cJSON_GetObjectItem(body_json, \"error\");\n        if (error_obj && cJSON_IsObject(error_obj)) {\n            cJSON *code = cJSON_GetObjectItem(error_obj, \"code\");\n            cJSON *domain = cJSON_GetObjectItem(error_obj, \"domain\");\n            cJSON *message = cJSON_GetObjectItem(error_obj, \"message\");\n\n            int err_code = code && cJSON_IsNumber(code) ? code->valueint : SC_ERR_UNKNOWN;\n            const char* err_domain = domain && cJSON_IsString(domain) ? domain->valuestring : \"unknown\";\n            const char* err_msg = message && cJSON_IsString(message) ? message->valuestring : \"Unknown error\";\n\n            /* Map domain string back to enum */\n            sc_service_domain_t domain_enum = SC_DOMAIN_UNKNOWN;\n            if (strcmp(err_domain, \"palette-service\") == 0) domain_enum = SC_DOMAIN_PALETTE;\n            else if (strcmp(err_domain, \"texture-service\") == 0) domain_enum = SC_DOMAIN_TEXTURE;\n            else if (strcmp(err_domain, \"audio-service\") == 0) domain_enum = SC_DOMAIN_AUDIO;\n            else if (strcmp(err_domain, \"narrative-service\") == 0) domain_enum = SC_DOMAIN_NARRATIVE;\n\n            response->error = sc_error_create(domain_enum, err_code, (int)http_status,\n                                              \"%s\", err_msg);\n            response->status = err_code;\n            return err_code;\n        }\n    }\n\n    response->status = SC_OK;\n    return SC_OK;\n}\n```\n\n#### Changes to `api-gateway/src/rest/fallback_handlers.c`\n\nUpdate to use structured errors:\n\n```c\n#include \"sc_errors.h\"\n\n/* Build error response from sc_error_t */\nstatic char*\nbuild_error_from_sc_error(const sc_error_t *err)\n{\n    if (!err) {\n        return build_error_payload(500, \"INTERNAL_ERROR\", \"Unknown error occurred\");\n    }\n\n    char iso[32];\n    iso8601_now(iso);\n\n    cJSON *root  = cJSON_CreateObject();\n    cJSON *error = cJSON_AddObjectToObject(root, \"error\");\n\n    cJSON_AddNumberToObject(error, \"code\", err->http_status_code);\n    cJSON_AddStringToObject(error, \"type\", sc_err_str(err->code));\n    cJSON_AddStringToObject(error, \"domain\", sc_error_get_domain_name(err->domain));\n    cJSON_AddStringToObject(error, \"message\", err->message ? err->message : \"No details\");\n    cJSON_AddStringToObject(error, \"timestamp\", iso);\n    cJSON_AddStringToObject(error, \"gateway\", SC_GATEWAY_VERSION);\n\n    char *json = cJSON_PrintUnformatted(root);\n    cJSON_Delete(root);\n    return json;\n}\n\n/* New handler for service errors */\nRestResponse\nrest_fallback_service_error(const RestRequest *req,\n                            const sc_error_t  *err)\n{\n    LOG_DEBUG(\"[REST] Service error handler for URI '%s': %s\",\n              req->uri, err ? err->message : \"null error\");\n\n    char *payload = build_error_from_sc_error(err);\n\n    RestResponse res = {\n        .status_code  = err ? err->http_status_code : 500,\n        .content_type = MIME_APP_JSON,\n        .body         = payload,\n        .body_len     = strlen(payload),\n        .must_free    = true\n    };\n    return res;\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n### 5. Errors\n\nErrors are created using `sc_error_create()` which allocates:\n1. The `sc_error_t` struct itself\n2. A copy of the formatted message string\n\n```c\nsc_error_t* err = sc_error_create(SC_DOMAIN_PALETTE, SC_ERR_DATA_NOT_FOUND, 404,\n                                  \"Palette with id %s not found\", id);\n```\n\n### Destroying Errors\n\nErrors must be destroyed when no longer needed to prevent memory leaks:\n\n```c\nif (err != NULL) {\n    /* Handle the error */\n    log_error(\"Error: %s\", err->message);\n\n    /* Destroy when done */\n    sc_error_destroy(err);\n}\n```\n\n### Error Propagation\n\nWhen propagating errors up the call stack, the caller takes ownership:\n\n```c\nsc_error_t* do_operation(void) {\n    sc_error_t* err = some_lower_level_call();\n    if (err != NULL) {\n        /* Add context and return - caller now owns the error */\n        return err;\n    }\n    return NULL;  /* Success */\n}\n```\n\n### Error Handling Pattern\n\nThe recommended pattern for consuming functions:\n\n```c\nvoid handle_request(Request* req, Response* resp) {\n    sc_error_t* err = service_operation(req->data);\n\n    if (err != NULL) {\n        /* Use error details to build response */\n        resp->status = err->http_status_code;\n        resp->body = format_error_json(err);\n\n        /* Destroy the error after use */\n        sc_error_destroy(err);\n        return;\n    }\n\n    /* Success path */\n    resp->status = 200;\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## Build Instructions\n\nAfter implementing all changes:\n\n```bash\n# From project root\nmkdir -p build && cd build\ncmake .. -DCMAKE_BUILD_TYPE=Debug -DSC_ENABLE_TESTS=ON\nmake -j$(nproc)\n\n# Run tests\nctest --output-on-failure\n```\n\nOr using the build script:\n\n```bash\n./scripts/build.sh --all --verbose\n```\n\n---\n\n## Summary of Changes by File\n\n| File | Changes **Traceability**: Error origin (domain) is always known\n3. **HTTP Mapping**: HTTP status codes are embedded in the error, eliminating ad-hoc mapping\n4. **Rich Messages**: Variadic message formatting allows detailed error descriptions\n5. **Memory Safety**: Clear ownership model with `sc_error_destroy()`\n6. **Gateway Integration**: Structured errors can be serialized directly to JSON responses\n7. **Testing**: Error assertions are more precise (check domain, code, HTTP status, message)\n\nThis refactoring provides a solid foundation for consistent error handling across the entire SynestheticCanvas microservice constellation.\n",

2. WRITE /logs/agent/solution.md
# Solution: Refactor Service-Level Error Handling into a Unified Common Library Abstraction

## Executive Summary

This document provides a complete solution for centralizing and standardizing error handling across the SynestheticCanvas microservice suite. The refactoring involves:

1. **Enhancing the Common Error Abstraction** in `libs/sc_common/`
2. **Refactoring the Palette Service** (`services/palette-service/`)
3. **Refactoring the Texture Service** (`services/texture-service/`)
4. **Updating the API Gateway** (`api-gateway/`)
5. **Updating Unit Tests**

## Analysis of Existing Error Handling

### Current State

After analyzing the codebase, I found the following error handling patterns:

1. **sc_common library** (`libs/sc_common/include/sc_errors.h`):
   - Already has an `sc_error_t` struct with `code`, `sys_err`, `msg`, `file`, `line`
   - Has an `sc_err_e` enumeration with comprehensive error codes
   - Has an `sc_err_to_http()` function that maps error codes to HTTP status codes
   - Uses macros like `SC_RAISE()` and `SC_TRY()` for error propagation
   - **Missing**: No service domain identification, no factory functions for dynamic error creation

2. **Palette Service** (`services/palette-service/`):
   - Uses `bool` return values for most functions
   - Has service-specific status enum `sc_ps_status_t` in the public header
   - Repository uses `palette_repo_status_t` enum
   - No unified error message propagation

3. **Texture Service** (`services/texture-service/`):
   - Uses `texture_service_status_t` enum
   - Repository uses integer codes (`REPO_OK`, `REPO_ERR_*`)
   - No unified error message propagation

4. **API Gateway** (`api-gateway/`):
   - Service client uses simple integer return codes
   - Fallback handlers generate JSON error responses manually
... (truncated)
